24 Mar 2017 00:37:36 : The Wild Weebs, general, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```py
def findPhrase(phrase):
    words = phrase.split(' ')
    Index = InvertedIndex[words[0]]
    if len(words) == 1:
        return Index
    ShorterPhrase = " ".join(words[1:])
    foundShorter = findPhrase(ShorterPhrase)
    foundLonger = {}
    for index in Index:
        for index2 in foundShorter:
            if index.Location + 1 == index2.Location and index.Scene == index2.Scene and index.Play == index2.Play:
                if words[0] in foundLonger.keys():
                    foundLonger[words[0]].append(index)
                else:
                    foundLonger[words[0]] = [index]
                break
    return foundLonger[words[0]]```
